The wording was extremely intense. Representatives of the Communist Trade Unions of Japan, China, and other countries all warmly guaranteed to assist Soviet Russia in defending its territory.

Important News

Increasing Japanese Troops 82

Third Division Arrives in Jilin and Heilongjiang

Hirose's Tenth Division Has Arrived

Eighth and Ninth Divisions Will Follow

National Salvation Army Headquarters Established in Suifenhe

A Brave and Capable Young Female Captain

Harbin Dispatch: The Japanese Army's Tenth Division from Himeji arrived in Harbin on the 18th. Its main force is still en route and is expected to arrive completely within ten to twelve days. The division commander is Lieutenant General Hirose, commanding four infantry regiments, two cavalry regiments, and one artillery regiment, totaling 16,000 personnel. In the future, except for three regiments remaining in Harbin, the rest will be deployed along the Harbin-Suifenhe railway line. Besides this division, the Eighth and Ninth Divisions will arrive in Jilin and Heilongjiang soon, together with the old Second Division, the Suzuki Mixed Brigade, and the Murai Mixed Brigade, reaching the Japanese plan of 75,000 troops. The commander of the Second Division, the Yokokawa Brigade, will go to the Jilin-Changchun railway line to take charge of the garrison, while the Amano Brigade will be stationed in Heilongjiang Province for a long time. The Japanese heavy troops gathering in Jilin and Heilongjiang are not only targeting us but also Russia. However, Japanese propaganda claims they will attack Ding Li's self-defense army and the National Salvation Army, and plan to use the first batch of ships dispatched when the river ice melts to transport Japanese soldiers to the lower reaches of the Songhua River to attack Yilan and Fujin. It is rumored that the newly arrived Eighth and Ninth Divisions will also be specifically assigned to this task. The self-defense army in the Yilan and Fujin area, with the support of Ma Zhanshan's army from eastern Heilongjiang, recovered Fangzheng County last week. It is now garrisoned by Chen Zongdai's troops. A small number of Japanese troops and Xi Qia's troops have retreated to Gaoli Maozi and Jiaxinzi. Xi Qia's troops are unwilling to kill each other; each soldier has both red and yellow armbands. When the self-defense army arrives, if they cannot retreat in time, they wear red armbands to show their allegiance. Therefore, the Japanese side deeply suspects that Xi Qia's troops have a tacit understanding with the Jilin army and are completely unreliable. The National Salvation Army on the eastern section of the Eastern Railway advanced to Shitouhezi on the 18th. The main force joined the Second Route led by Liu Wankui and moved towards Gaolingzi. Xi Qia's troops retreated to Weishahe, relying on the assistance of Japanese troops from Yimianpo to form a front line. On the 18th, the railway tracks between Dadaohezi and Shitouhezi stations were dismantled by Xi Qia's troops to prevent the advance of the National Salvation Army, so the National Salvation Army is currently stationed in that area. The Japanese Army's Murai Brigade is constructing defensive works in the southern mountains of Yimianpo to prevent the National Salvation Army from attacking. Vehicles on the Harbin-Suifenhe railway line are frequently delayed due to the advances and retreats of the National Salvation Army and the Japanese army. Wang Delin's National Salvation Army headquarters has recently moved to Suifenhe. Its commando teams are still active near Yanji. The International Youth Army is expanding its organization by contacting Koreans and Japanese, echoing Wang's army. The Japanese side fears that deeper incursions will be unfavorable, and because the area is on the Russian border, it is easy to have direct conflicts with Russia, so they are only deploying troops between Erdaogou and Longjingcun. Recently, they also transferred an air force team to be stationed there permanently for assistance. From Yimianpo to Suifenhe, local officials and tax authorities are being replaced by the National Salvation Army. All politics are in order, and the people love the National Salvation Army. They also provide special protection for the Eastern Railway traffic. Passengers traveling there do not feel any danger. A branch headquarters of the National Salvation Army is located in Hengdaohe, with a captain who is a beautiful young woman, wearing a blue silk shirt, carrying a Mauser pistol, often riding a horse through the streets, extremely brave and capable, and the soldiers are very respectful to her. The Japanese side claims that she is from Soviet Russia and graduated from the Far East International Military and Political School. (19th)

Implementing Opium Public Sales in Hebei, Shanxi, and Chahar 85

Levying a Heavy Tax to Replenish Military Expenses

Official Circles Claim to "Prohibit Through Taxation"

Tianjin Dispatch: When Anhui, Henan, Hubei and other provinces opened up opium prohibition and established taxation bureaus in the past, those in the North with a desire for profit were extremely envious. They repeatedly agitated for the public sale of opium in North China. Gu Zhang Xueliang expressed his opposition. The Hebei Provincial Civil Affairs Director Wang Yuke also once said to others, "I only have one son. I will never do anything unethical." Unexpectedly, after the September 18th Incident, the Northeast Army obeyed the order of non-resistance and successively withdrew into the pass, with no fewer than 200,000 people. In the past, the military expenses were shared by Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Hebei, and Chahar, and assisted by the Central Government. With the national crisis, the central government's finances were extremely stretched and no longer assisted. Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces were also occupied by the Japanese army. After Hebei and Chahar provinces abolished likin, the provincial treasury revenue sharply declined. Although taxes such as business production and sales were used to compensate, it was only about one-third of the previous likin revenue. Expenses for political and educational construction were already insufficient. Now, suddenly adding military expenses for 100,000 to 200,000 people, how can they bear it? Therefore, the Beiping Financial Reorganization Committee was born in response to the times. The so-called reorganization is that no matter how difficult each agency is, they are required to raise a certain amount of military expenses every month. Therefore, each agency only has one way: to reduce salaries and report effectiveness. At first, 80% of the salary was issued, and then 80% of 80% was issued, so in reality, only 65% was issued. For clerks and secretaries with a monthly salary of 20 yuan, the actual amount received each month was 13 yuan. It is not even enough for personal food, let alone supporting a family. However, even with such austerity, the amount saved is still not enough to cover the military's expenses, resulting in arrears in pay for several months. The armed ranks have raised difficulties one after another, even threatening to refuse to be responsible if wages are not paid. The provincial and municipal authorities lack the ability to make money, and there have been angry remarks about suspending the payment of political and educational construction expenses (party fees are of course excluded) to pay for military expenses. Unexpectedly, they actually went ahead and publicly sold opium.

Recently, Yan Xishan rectified Shanxi's administration, believing that the people of Shanxi were too deeply addicted to opium, spending more than 50 million yuan each year. To gradually eliminate the poison, he implemented the official sale of anti-smoking medicine. This anti-smoking medicine uses opium paste as the main raw material. It is estimated that it can generate 20 million yuan in profit each year to be used for military and political construction expenses. The Hebei provincial authorities, upon hearing this, were greatly envious and also proceeded with the public sale of opium. Zhang Xueliang, due to financial difficulties for military expenses, expressed his tacit approval. However, Hebei Province had long since ceased the cultivation of poppies. Blacklisted goods come from Chahar and Rehe provinces. To ensure that the source is unobstructed and the benefits are shared equally, Hebei, Chahar, and Suiyuan provinces simultaneously implemented public sales. The Rehe provincial authorities have other methods and did not implement the same system. However, the name "public sale of opium" is not elegant, so it is euphemistically called "prohibit through taxation," establishing bureaus and issuing [destruction certificates]. The brewing and maturity of this matter took only ten days, because it was feared that public opinion would be against it, so it was carried out secretly and very quickly. The names of those in charge have not yet been announced, but it is known that the traffickers are all "tigers wearing hats." Real opium traffickers mostly failed to join. In Tianjin, the Northern Company has been established, with capital of an unknown amount, but it is known that a total of more than 3,000 tons of goods have been transported to the Dongkou and Beikou ports, which can be described as shocking. There are also many transporters in transit. The public sale locations in Hebei Province that have been decided are Tianjin, Beiping, Tangshan, Tanggu, Shanhaiguan, Baoding, Shijiazhuang, and Daming, which will be gradually expanded in the future. As far as Hebei Province is concerned, the annual tax is estimated to reach 30 million yuan. It has now been decided to implement public sales on May 1st. After this, anyone who does not affix a destruction certificate will be considered a criminal and arrested. In recent days, soil prices have fallen sharply because there is too much inventory in the concessions, and everyone wants to sell it before the public sale period. However, in the future, major soil traffickers in the concessions will have no way to smuggle it, and there will be many people who will lose their jobs due to the public sale.

Yesterday, the military, police, and gendarmerie agencies in this city received an order from their superiors to investigate and punish private transportation of drugs, with the following content: (1) Gendarmes, police, and road police who seize drugs that have not been affixed with a destruction certificate will be sent to the Drug Prohibition Committee for summary destruction. (2) For the private transportation of drugs mentioned above, one-third of the value estimated by the committee will be used as a cash reward to encourage them. (3) Those who are completely arrested by the gendarmes, police, and road police will receive the full amount of the reward. (4) Those who are arrested after being reported by someone will receive half of the reward for the informer and the gendarmerie/police, respectively. If two or more groups of agencies simultaneously discover or arrest someone, they should share the reward equally. (5) Anyone has the right to report the drugs mentioned above. Those who report should report to the gendarmerie/police in the jurisdiction, and the agency receiving the report should immediately cooperate with the gendarmerie/police to search and arrest them according to the law. (6) Those who make false reports will be fined between 100 and 1,000 yuan. (April 24th)

Gradually Eliminating Bandits in Southern Shandong 86

Zhang Heilian's Troops Flee to Linyi

People in Shandong Suggest Developing Mengshan

Jinan Dispatch: The bandits Zhang Heilian, Wang Changyou, Yang Guangsheng, Shi Zengfu, and others in southern Shandong were surrounded and severely suppressed by Xie Shuxian, the commander of the southern Shandong militia, leading the militias of Mengyin and Yishui counties, together with the 244th Brigade of Yun Qichang stationed in Yishui. Except for Shi Zengfu, who has already returned to righteousness and was organized as a southern Shandong militia under control,

Zhang Heilian, Wang Changyou, and others fled to Jishan. Yang Guangsheng fled to Niutougu. Soon, Yang Guangsheng was arrested and executed. His troops lost their leader. The headquarters of the southern Shandong militia then ordered the directly subordinate mixed regiment and Shi Zengfu's troops to

Swiftly and fiercely suppress them. On the 20th, the troops were completely defeated, and Yang Guangsheng's parents, wife, and children, as well as thirteen important bandit leaders, were captured. Yang's head has been escorted to the Tai'an County government. Zhang Heilian, Wang Changyou, and others, who were hiding in Jishan, have now fled to the mountains in the boundary of Linyi due to their isolated and weak forces. The commander of the 81st Division stationed in Linyi, Zhan Shutang, will lead his troops to suppress them. Xie Shuxian, the commander of the southern Shandong militia, specially sent Wang Chenmian, the regimental adjutant of his directly subordinate mixed regiment, to Jinan from Xintai at 9:30 yesterday (the 23rd) to report on the recent situation of suppressing bandits. He immediately went to the provincial government to meet with Han Fuju to report on the situation of suppressing Zhang Heilian, Yang Guangsheng, and others, and to ask for

Instructions on how to deal with the captured relatives of Yang Guangsheng. It is said that after Wang met with Han, he was ordered to execute Yang's head and thirteen bandits and display their heads in Tai'an as a warning to the public.

Mengshan in southern Shandong stretches for hundreds of miles, deep and dangerous, with few people. In the past twenty years, it has become a bandit den, making suppression very difficult. The people in hundreds of villages near Mengshan have fled, leaving no one. In the past two years, after repeated suppression, it has gradually been cleared. The mountains are rich in resources. Not only are there inexhaustible mineral and timber resources, but it can also be used as a vast pasture. It is truly a major

Mysterious treasure trove in southern Shandong. Hou Zunzhao, a former lieutenant colonel staff officer of the southern Shandong militia headquarters, who knows the situation in the mountains of southern Shandong, recently submitted a petition to the provincial government, requesting that the Mengshan resources be developed by the militia to combine soldiers and farmers. The content of his petition is roughly as follows: (1) There are more than 300 villages near Mengshan with no one, and most of the fertile land is barren. Therefore, the land tax in Fei, Meng, and Ding counties has been reduced by four-tenths, and the number of people migrating has been reduced by three-tenths. If Mengshan can be developed, the displaced people will return to their homes and cultivate their land, and the land tax will return to its old rules, increasing revenue by 70,000 to 80,000 yuan each year. Not only will industry develop and forestry flourish, but the scenic spots will also be improved. (2) Historically, opening mines and developing wasteland requires huge sums of money. In this difficult time, it is difficult to raise money to proceed. It is planned to use the southern Shandong militia as the backbone of the development, implementing the policy of turning soldiers into workers and combining soldiers and farmers. If the provincial treasury adds working equipment, it can be handled. (3) Although there are many trees in Mengshan, no one is in charge, and people are allowed to cut them down, making prevention difficult. After development, a large-scale forest farm can be planned, which can help the country's wealth. (4) Our country is based on agriculture, with many people and little land in the interior. Over the years, people from Zhili and Shandong have gone to the Northeast to reclaim land, showing that the people are rich in agriculture. Since Mengshan has been developed, the fertile land without people can be sold at official prices, so that the land tax can be returned. The newly developed official property can also be priced to the people and taxed according to law. Since the incidents in the Northeast, the number of farmers going to the Northeast has decreased sharply. Mengshan is located in central Shandong, compared with those who travel thousands of miles to buy land and reclaim it in the Northeast, the advantages and disadvantages of distance are obvious. (5) Take the materials, stone, and soil of Mengshan and set up kilns on the spot to burn lime bricks and tiles, and sell them to farmers at low prices, so that the old villages with few people can be easily rebuilt. The wood of Mengshan can be used as rafters, pillars, and beams, and can also be sold to the people at low prices, so that villages can be easily formed. (6) After Mengshan is developed, cattle can be raised to benefit farmers' cultivation, sheep can be raised to benefit farmers' clothing, chickens can be raised to benefit farmers' food, and there are many beehives in Mengshan, which can be expanded to raise bees. Mengshan has water and can also raise fish. There are many foxes in the mountains, which are considered excellent. (7) Honeysuckle and Polygonum multiflorum are the main products of Mengshan, and other medicinal products can also be planted. Mengshan also produces tea, which is very cool and can treat fire diseases. As for flowers, bamboo, and tea, they can also be planted according to the local conditions. (8) Fei has silver mines, and Meng has coal mines, which can be mined one after another. (9) Historically, the strategy of enriching the country has been mainly to generate profits. The various sources of profit mentioned above are somewhat helpful. Now that the banditry has been cleared, the progress is timely. The procedures for proceeding are to first build the main road to Mengshan to facilitate the people's movement, set up kilns to burn bricks and tiles to facilitate the people's housing, and divide and measure the land to facilitate the people's cultivation. All

These plans and management can belong to the Department of Construction, and the required labor can be taken from the southern Shandong militia. If there are bandits, they will be suppressed. If there is no labor, they will work. Progress will be gradual, and the matter can be accomplished. If so, the southern Shandong militia will benefit the people, and the benefits will be great. (24th)

Second Yin Ruins Discovered in Junxian 87

Anyang Dispatch: Since last year's case of officials and civilians colluding to steal cultural relics in Xin Village, northwestern Junxian, the Henan Provincial Government detained and prosecuted County Magistrate Zeng Liangdong and strictly ordered the arrest of the fugitives. In order to preserve the cultural relics, the Academia Sinica and the Henan Provincial Government specially formulated eight articles on the method of jointly organizing the Antiquities Research Association and designated Xin Village in Junxian as a pilot area. The Research Association then sent member Guo Baojun to Junxian with Ma Yuancai, a representative of the Henan Provincial Government, to prepare for excavation. Guo and others arrived in Junxian on the 12th of this month. County Magistrate Li Shude of Junxian was ordered in advance to send 30 security team members to protect the village. On the 13th, Guo and others also arrived in the village with County Magistrate Li. On the 16th, work officially began, with dozens of workers. Many cultural relics have been unearthed successively,

Such as stone axes, shell knives, sickles, divination bones, tiles, cooking pots, bronze arrowheads, stone arrowheads, bone arrowheads, and bone saws, all of which are very similar to those unearthed in Xiaotun, Anyang. There is also a section of rammed earth in the southwest, which is especially distinctive. The northern section of the rammed earth was already exposed in the past, with a total of more than 40 layers visible, 6 meters high, about 16 meters long, and about 4 meters wide. Its southwest is covered by a thick layer of loess. The boundary between the loess layer and the rammed earth is obvious. The east wall of the rammed earth is mostly filled with gray soil, which is level with the rammed earth. Most of the cultural relics come from it. There are also rammed earth remains in the north field, about 15 meters long, and the edge has not yet been seen. Each layer is about 0.05 meters thick, slightly different from the above-mentioned thickness of 0.15 meters to 0.2 meters. According to Guo and others, it was rumored last year that this place was the Yin Dynasty mausoleum, but according to the excavation situation in recent days, no definite evidence has been obtained. However, judging from the shape of the unearthed objects and the condition of the strata, it can be asserted that this place is a residential site of the Yin people. As for whether the Yin Dynasty mausoleum is also in this place, one dare not arbitrarily determine it without more abundant materials. (21st)

Investigation and Reporting of Disaster Situation in Eastern Henan 88

Many People in Various Counties Starved to Death

Kaifeng Dispatch: The terrain in eastern Henan is low-lying, and the flood disaster is particularly severe. Although relief has been provided several times, many people have been saved. However, in this famine spring, when the old grain has run out and the new grain has not yet arrived, disaster reports and requests for relief from various counties are pouring in. The Provincial Relief Association has specially sent Wang Yinghou and others to various counties with severe disasters to investigate the disaster situation in order to find ways to provide relief. At this moment, the members have completed the investigation of the disaster situation in six counties in eastern Henan and reported to the Relief Association. The overview

Is as follows: (1) In Xiayi County, the flood receded relatively late last year, and only five-tenths of the wheat was planted. About one-third of the wheat was dug up and eaten by the disaster-stricken people this spring. Recently, strong winds have repeatedly occurred, causing the wheat seedlings to turn yellow and wither, and the tree buds to wither and fall. Emaciated women and children compete to collect tree leaves as if they were vying for a prize. However, after door-to-door investigations, all families are found to be empty and the stoves are cold. Most people fill their stomachs with leaves, and some mix sorghum hulls to make cakes for food, but it is only eaten once a day or every other day. The situation is the same in other areas, and the misery is indescribable. (2) In Yongcheng County, the northeast two, eight, and nine districts had very little wheat harvest last year, and the autumn was flooded. Because the flood receded relatively late, not enough wheat was planted. The spring was dry, and many seedlings withered. The market price of wheat and beans is 550 wen per catty, and sorghum is 455 wen. Grain prices are extremely high,

Unprecedented. Emaciated people gather in groups to collect wheat seedlings and bark to fill their stomachs. The county government has announced a ban on eating wheat seedlings, but it cannot be stopped. The danger to people's lives can be imagined. (3) In Zhecheng County, the first district, beggars fill the streets in the city. Three abandoned children were found crying for their parents, and one disaster-stricken person starved to death. The relief distribution association has not yet buried them. There are those who carry cypress bark, elm leaves, willow leaves, and sweet potato vines to sell as food. In Dongguan, agricultural implements and utensils are displayed on the street, all sold at reduced prices. More than a thousand disaster-stricken people gather in the Taiyi Temple in Xiguan, and many have died of the seasonal epidemic. According to Li Yongchun, the town leader of Cishengji Town in the second district, Zhang Chun, Liu Xing, and 13 others in the town have starved to death one after another. Zhang Jingxian, the brigade commander, reported that Zhang Xiaoxian and 7 other starving people in the village died of starvation, two young women fled, and countless people became beggars. In the third district, the investigation team saw that the town leader Yang Quanwen was burying disaster-stricken people who had starved to death and said that Yang Xixing and 9 others had starved to death in the town this spring, 5 women had fled, and countless people had become beggars. Moreover, Wang Daochun and 3 others were burned to death and Wang Daomei and 4 others were killed by Li Gongcheng's bandits at the Kaihuangdian Store. Wang Zhongbo and 3 others were kidnapped, and 372 houses were burned, leaving thousands of refugees homeless. The disaster in the fourth district is particularly severe. Every family hears the sound of hunger, and every day people starve to death. Zhang Youdao, a Confucian scholar in Qitaishi Town, committed suicide due to starvation. Lu Yingfa, a wealthy household in Lu Guanmiao Village, had his stored grain divided up and eaten by starving people and committed suicide by jumping into a well with his wife due to starvation. There is a slave market in Hong'enji, and 1,043 houses were burned and 42 people were killed in 18 villages in Xuankou Township by Li Gongcheng. There are also groups of three or five robbing grain and intercepting vehicles, so grain trucks dare not enter the territory. In this time of famine, it is easiest to cause chaos, which has a great impact on local security. The investigation team has consulted with County Magistrate Zhu to find ways to prevent it. (4) In Luyi County, the Liu Huitang family in Liu Wafang Village in the first district committed suicide due to starvation. In the second and third districts, there are almost no people. There are only people with pale faces who are almost blown down by the wind, crawling on the road in groups of four or five. The misery in the two districts is especially severe. Wang, the wife of Sun Lianzhong in Wa Sun Village, had a son who was only four years old and kept crying from hunger. Wang had no way to survive and threw herself into a well to die. Wang Shuang in Qiuquji abandoned his son on the side of the village because his wife had already starved to death and was picked up by the village chief. Wang Shuang traveled to Xiaolizhuang, about ten miles north, and threw himself into a well to die. Li Zicheng's family of three in Liwa Village in the fourth district committed suicide by throwing themselves into the river together. The disaster situation in the sixth, seventh, and eighth districts is similar to that of other districts, but they are more severely ravaged by bandits than other districts. (5) The residents along the Nihe River, twenty miles south of Xiangcheng County, rely entirely on aquatic plants, snails, grass roots, and bark for sustenance. Two people starved to death in Ma Tinglan's family in Malaozhuang, one starved to death in Ma Mao's family, one starved to death in Ma Enzan's family, one starved to death in Ma Nao's family, one starved to death in Lu Zhenlun's family, one starved to death in Zhang Hao's family, one starved to death in Hou Jin Yang's family, and Qiu Ma died of starvation. (6) The disaster situation in Shenqiu County is even more severe. The rich have become destitute, and the poor have become starving corpses. Wild vegetables, bark, aquatic plants, and snails have long been exhausted. Emaciated people are heard crying from hunger along the way. In Xu Lizhuang and other places in the sixth district, nine people, including Lu Zhuo, starved to

Death. In Ximen Village in the first district, three people, including Yang Laoda, starved to death. In Wanglaojia Village in the second district, one Wang Daniu starved to death. In the third district, 16 people, including Li Jianyin, starved to death. The rest are also waiting to be fed and are on the verge of death.

Guizhou Construction Department Surveys and Measures the Huangguoshu Hydropower Plant 89

Guiyang Dispatch: In order to prepare for the construction of the Guiyang Shuikousi Hydropower Plant, the Guizhou Provincial Department of Construction recently hired engineer Xu Kuannian from Shanghai to come to Guizhou to design it. After Xu arrived in the province, the director of the department, Ju Ren, accompanied engineer Xu, the director of the Electricity Bureau, Yu Pengsen, and the department's technical personnel, Hua Laifeng, Zhang Gengrong, Luo Youmei, Li Shuheng, Xie Zimei, and Li Yifeng, to Huangguoshu to conduct on-site surveys and measurements. As a result, according to engineer Xu's report, the Huangguoshu Waterfall has a head of 210 feet. The cross-section downstream of the waterfall is 137 feet wide, 9 feet at the deepest point, and the average flow rate is about 2 and 3/4 inches per second, resulting in a flow rate of 184 cubic feet per second. If water pipes are used to divert water to the turbine, it can generate 3,000 horsepower all day long. If the purpose is only to supply electricity for lighting and it is assumed to be used for ten hours a day, the water power can be increased to 7,200 horsepower. If electricity is sent to the place of use and it is still calculated as being used for ten hours a day, the actual usable power is about 3,700 kilowatts. Based on 40 light bulbs per kilowatt, the water power obtained during the measurement of Huangguoshu can light 150,000 bulbs.

XuZhou Disaster Victims Crowd 90

Xuzhou correspondence: Xubu suffered unusually severe flooding last summer. A flood relief association was established by various sectors to carry out relief efforts. However, after winter, as time passed, the authorities inevitably became less enthusiastic about disaster relief. Now, in the spring famine, there are many disaster victims in the area, especially in rural areas where transportation is inconvenient and food is scarce, leading to widespread starvation. In the urban areas, due to easier transportation, disaster victims from all directions have gathered, resulting in roads filled with displaced people. The Relief Branch Association has been handling relief distribution and has requested Mr. Zhu Ziqiao to allocate 100 tons of red grain. A few days ago, Mr. Zhu sent Zhang Yuting and Wang Guolin to transport it from Ping to Xuzhou. The Relief Branch Association is organizing investigations and distribution in the surrounding villages. The Xuzhou Red Swastika Society is also separately handling the distribution of flour, setting up porridge kitchens, and organizing price controls, but these efforts are like a drop in the bucket and difficult to make widespread. The Jinpu Railway Garrison Headquarters, concerned that the large number of disaster victims might affect public order, yesterday specifically instructed Chen Xueshun, the head of the military police and police department, and Yang Wei, the magistrate of Tongshan County, to quickly devise ways to eliminate the problem. The order stated, "Last year's floods affected various provinces, and disaster victims from all directions are displaced. Xuzhou is a strategic location, and more and more people are coming here. They are leading the old and carrying the young, begging for food from door to door, enduring the wind and dew. It's extremely tragic. Although there are relief organizations and charitable groups in Xuzhou City, they do not investigate and register the refugees' movements, nor do they find ways to send them away. The number of people increases daily without limit. Providing a fixed amount of relief grain to an unlimited number of refugees yields little effect and creates greater problems. Recently, refugees have gathered in the city, forming groups and begging from door to door. There are even starving people on the roads, which is not only unsightly but also inhumane. Those in charge of local administration should take immediate action. Moreover, as the number of displaced people increases daily, the weak are abandoned in ditches, which is pitiable, while the strong resort to desperate measures, which is likely to affect public order. If we do not quickly devise ways to eliminate this problem, the consequences will be unimaginable. Therefore, we order the heads of the department and the county to jointly supervise the local police to conduct thorough investigations and registration of the number of refugees entering the area, and to convene relief organizations and charitable groups to earnestly discuss ways to accommodate, relieve, and send them away. This must be implemented within a specified period. Special attention should be paid to the repatriation aspect to ensure that disaster victims from all areas do not gather in one city, creating a hidden danger for the local area. We hereby set a deadline of five days from the receipt of this order to determine a solution, and ten days to implement it effectively. As this matter concerns local public order, the heads of the department and the county must work hard and take responsibility for handling it, and must not procrastinate or cause delays, which will incur punishment. They should also report on the progress of implementation at any time for verification." The two agencies, after receiving the order, immediately proceeded to handle the matter. However, while disaster relief requires the unreserved efforts of all parties, it is also important to address the root cause. Dredging rivers and using labor in place of relief were pre-planned by last year's flood relief association. Therefore, the local authorities should pay even more attention to this." (23rd)

The Rural Education Department of Lida High School Suffers a Terrible Robbery 94

Losses Reach More Than 46,000 Yuan

The school buildings of Shanghai Lida Academy were originally divided into two parts. One was located on Lida Road in Jiangwan, Shanghai, for the junior high school and the general course of the high school. It was completely destroyed when the Japanese army attacked Jiangwan. Details have been published in various newspapers. The other was located in Nanxiang, Jiading, for the rural education department of the high school, located south of the Jinghu Railway, about seven miles away from the Nanxiang train station. It covers an area of more than 160 mu, with a fish pond of 25 mu in the middle. The school building is built next to the pond, with excellent scenery. To the northwest of the school building is a chicken farm, with four modern chicken coops that can raise more than 2,500 chickens. To the south of the school building is a bee farm, to the west is a cotton seed improvement area and a horticultural area, and the rest is wheat and rice fields. Usually, all production activities are operated by the student-teacher co-organized work-study society. In addition to raising chickens, bees, and fish, they also engage in cultivation. Therefore, the production gained is enough to meet the needs of students' learning. After our army changed its strategy and withdrew from the first line of defense, the Japanese army occupied Nanxiang. First, they slaughtered all the chickens, sheep, rabbits, and farming cattle raised by the school. The rice and wheat grains were looted. Then they destroyed the school building horizontally. The bee farm and bee colony were destroyed. According to an on-the-spot investigation, the storage room, shed, cattle shed, and grass shed north of the school building have been burned to the ground. The meeting hall, chicken feed room, kitchen, farm buildings, and farm tool room have all been pried open and destroyed. The bricks and tiles are in a mess, and the situation is very miserable. The chicken coops and greenhouses in the northwest of the school building have been dismantled, and the wood, glass, and wire mesh have all been transported away. The large and small boats and motor drain pumps parked in the schoolyard have all been robbed. The indoor utensils have been completely destroyed. Even the bamboo fences, doors, windows, and floors have not been spared. The total property loss has reached more than 46,000 yuan. The Academy founded the rural education department originally to improve rural culture and improve the lives of farmers. It was a long and arduous road, but it had just begun to take shape. It was planned to add a compulsory primary school to prevent poor young people in the vicinity from losing their schooling. How could the barbaric Japanese army have used all means to destroy our country's cultural institutions? The school was located in a remote rural area, but unfortunately suffered this terrible robbery.

Score 1000 to 750

Although Li Gongying Lost Momentum Yesterday, Hope for Victory Remains Shanghai International Advanced Shooting Competition, yesterday was the first day of the finals. Department Approves Flexibility in Sugar Tax 100

Result of Representatives Going to Beijing

The Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, previously due to the Jianghai Customs announcement, following an order from the Ministry of Finance, to implement new sugar tax rates starting April 1st, and using polarimetric testing as the standard for classification. The industry had previously ordered 500,000 dan of red and white sugar from Java and other places for February and March. Due to the Shanghai war, following the Chamber of Commerce's notice, letters were sent to various foreign firms to delay loading. Therefore, only partial shipments have not yet returned to Shanghai. If the newly established tax rates are applied, there would be a sudden increase of more than four taels. The sugar for which foreign firms were asked to delay loading would, after arriving in Shanghai, incur more tax than before, which is truly difficult to bear in the current situation. Moreover, the new tax regulations have as many as fourteen categories, with tax rates differing by as much as two yuan per dan of customs duty, making it complex, cumbersome, and unbearable. Sugar taxes worldwide, in East Asian countries, mostly use the Dutch standard for classification. Although European and American countries use degrees as the basis, they only differentiate between raw materials and finished products, with absolutely no division into as many as fourteen categories. It was requested that the classification standard be changed to one category for below 90 degrees, one category for 91 to 96 degrees, and another category for above 97 degrees, etc. This was submitted by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the Ministries of Finance and Industry, requesting adoption and implementation. Subsequently, the association further stated that if the Ministry of Finance increased the sugar tax to protect domestic sugar, then the quantity of sugar produced in our country has decreased in recent years, and is not even sufficient to supply one corner of the country, relying entirely on imported goods to make up the difference. Moreover, sugar is needed for flavoring and cooking, and has become a necessary item for the people. The floods have just subsided, followed by the Japanese disaster. Increasing the sugar tax will only make the people's livelihood more difficult. In terms of commerce, the sugar trade has very thin profits, with peacetime earnings only reaching five per thousand. This time, the 500,000 dan of sugar with delayed loading will require additional tax payments. According to established practice on the foreign firm side, foreign taxes are usually borne externally. When the sugar industry resells to trading houses, it includes the tax. This kind of newly increased tax is truly impossible to recoup. Moreover, there are many categories of imported goods, but the increase only applies to the sugar tax. The value of each dan of white sugar is only about six taels, but the tax is as high as more than eight taels. No other goods have such a heavy tax. Upon the request of the sugar industry, the standing committee meeting of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce publicly appointed Standing Committee member Wang Yansong, along with industry representative Zheng Zenan and others, to go to Beijing to present the actual situation to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government, requesting a temporary suspension of implementation. The petition representatives have completed their work and returned to Shanghai last night. It is heard that the relevant departments and courts have all understood the difficulties of the sugar industry and agreed to make adjustments. As for the report in yesterday's newspaper stating that the Ministry of Finance had not approved the extension, it was still a reply to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's telegram before the petition representatives arrived in Beijing, and not the result of the representatives' petition, etc.

Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to the Public Works Department Regarding Electricity Fees 101

Electricity Fees Should Be Based on Actual Usage

Deposit Reduced by One-Third

The Shanghai Settlement Taxpayers' Association yesterday sent a letter to the Secretary of the Public Works Department, stating: "Dear Sir, According to Wang Xinfu's letter, the electricity bill for this month from the power company states that 12 degrees of electricity were used, totaling three taels, seven mace, and five fen of silver, etc. According to this calculation, the power company has clearly implemented a measure to increase the minimum monthly electricity fee by two times. Recently, we have seen in the newspapers that your association is negotiating with the Public Works Department regarding this matter. Therefore, we are sending this special letter to inquire whether our electricity fee should be paid according to the new rate before the negotiations are properly handled. We also request that your association first send a letter to the Public Works Department, instructing them to immediately inform the power company that for all users who delay payment due to the unresolved issue, the electricity supply should not be cut off, to avoid inconvenience, etc." After investigation, regarding the new electricity fee regulations, this association has sent a letter requesting rectification. According to the letter, the electricity fee for 12 degrees should only be one tael and four mace and four fen of silver based on the current rate. Now, it is required to pay three taels, seven mace, and five fen of silver, which means that people are bearing an obligation of two taels and three mace and one fen of silver without any rights. This kind of new regulation causes ordinary people to suffer uncompensated losses. If calculated by ten thousand households, the Shanghai Power Company can obtain 23,100 taels of silver per month without providing electricity, and 277,200 taels of silver per year. At seven mace and two fen per national currency, it would be 385,000 yuan. This kind of new regulation is unreasonable in terms of legal principles and has drawbacks in reality. Furthermore, the French Concession's electricity fees are based on actual usage, with no so-called minimum fee. We truly do not know why your bureau approved this kind of regulation. Moreover, recently, the Shanghai Power Company has changed to collecting electricity fees once a month, unlike when your bureau handled it, collecting every three months. Why is the deposit not immediately refunded by two-thirds? In other words, why is the deposit collected based on more than one month's estimated usage? This association believes that the above two methods benefit the company and harm the users, which is contrary to legal principles and lacks a basis for fairness. Accordingly, we send this letter requesting that the Shanghai Power Company promptly change these new regulations: (1) Electricity fees should be based on actual usage; (2) The deposit should be reduced to one-third as before when it was collected every three months. We hope you will investigate and handle accordingly."

Part of it is for Japanese Military Rations Japanese merchants recently purchased a large quantity of wheat from Australia, and two batches have been shipped to Shanghai. When the wheat arrived in Shanghai, the Japanese merchants did not dare to unload it themselves and entrusted a Chinese customs broker to transport it ashore. It is heard that part of this Australian wheat is used as military rations.

Shipped in Batches to Shanghai Shanghai Chinese flour mills have purchased a large quantity of wheat from Australia, and the following have already been shipped to Shanghai: 95,078 bags transported by the Esmoore, 106,242 bags transported by the Avistone, 106,480 bags carried by the Indian City, 7,801 tons carried by the Ballarun, and 8,973 tons carried by the Shelkhula. It is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai in the next two days.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Reduced Tax Collection for Tobacco and Alcohol Licenses 109

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Nanjing Ministry of Finance and the Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol yesterday, stating: "To the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol: On the 25th of this month, the Shanghai Tobacco Industry, Fen Wine Industry, Shaoxing Wine Industry, and Tobacco Leaf Industry Associations jointly stated in a letter that due to the impact of the Shanghai war, commerce has been suspended. Our association has jointly submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance and the Provincial Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol, requesting exemption from the summer tobacco and alcohol license tax for this year to alleviate the difficulties of businesses, etc. The ministry replied that after investigating, Shangbao County experienced commercial impact due to the war, which is a fact. However, tobacco and alcohol licenses are taxes levied on business operations. All tobacco and alcohol shops, except those that are closed and exempt from taxation, should follow the regulations and obtain licenses. There is no precedent for exemption due to circumstances, and the request cannot be approved. Please take note of this reply. The provincial bureau also replied, stating that the impact of the war is only temporary, and the request to exempt the summer license tax cannot be approved. Please take note of this reply. We received this reply after a little over a month. The spring tax collection period began on January 1st, and most (70-80 percent) had already completed their tax payments before the January 28th incident occurred. The businesses were only operating for slightly over one month before the incident. Moreover, it is customary to settle accounts at the end of the year, and people have been displaced and are suffering greatly. Although some are forced to reopen their businesses now, they have been idle for a long time, and their capital has been depleted. Some hope to collect accounts receivable to prepare for closure, while others are working hard to maintain the business to feed their families. They cannot stop if they want to. In the end, business is still bleak. Under these circumstances, it would not be excessive for the government to show love for the people and issue currency to provide relief. Our association does not dare to make this request because we are well aware of the inadequate state of the national treasury. Therefore, we only request exemption from the summer license tax. Unexpectedly, the Ministry of Finance believes that there is no precedent to follow and refuses to approve the request. However, the Japanese invasion is also an extraordinary event. Merchants would not complain unless they were truly in dire straits. Alas, our merchants have no way to complain, and the tax collectors have a superficial view, thinking that since the shops have reopened, they are sending out tax collectors everywhere to intimidate and scare people under the guise of heavy national taxes. They do not ask about the content of the business or anything else. They only know how to drain the pond to catch all the fish, regardless of the people's plight. It is also heard that the spring tax collected by the bureau did not reach three-tenths of the original amount submitted to the province. Why is the government favoring the contractors (i.e., the tax collectors) while being harsh on the merchants after the disaster? Our association witnesses the difficulties of the merchants and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we specially send this letter to your bureau for review and request that you forward it to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Finance's Stamp Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol. Since it is difficult to completely waive all taxes, please allow reduced tax collection so that both national taxes and business conditions can be taken care of. Once the overall situation returns to normal, it will still be handled according to the previous regulations, etc. According to this, since the merchants in Shangbao County have been affected by the war since the January 28th incident, the stagnation of their tobacco and alcohol business is a fact that cannot be concealed. Such an extraordinary event, those in charge of taxation should not be stubborn due to lack of precedent, and insist on scraping. Furthermore, according to reports, the spring tax submitted to the province is less than 30% of the full amount. The provincial treasury has limited income, but the tax collection bureau is still taxing as usual, giving it an opportunity to profit. Why is the government better to them than to the merchants? Now, after the merchant had requested exemption for the summer license tax, it was not approved. As such, they are forced to ask for reduced tax, and it is stated that once the overall situation returns to normal, the regulations will still be followed as normal. They are taking public tax collection into account, even while asking for reduced burden. Your ministry and bureau should be considerate of the businesses and no longer reject them on set rules, which will leave them voiceless. We request this in the telegram and hope it will be approved, as it will be for public convenience. Sincerely, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Shen Zhuowu's Remains Were Entombed Yesterday 112

Memorial Service to be Held at the Jade Buddha Temple on the 30th

Shen Zhuowu, manager of the China Evening News, unfortunately encountered an accident on the Dada Company's Dade ship while heading to Jiangbei to preside over disaster relief efforts last year at Qiwangsha. It has been over one hundred and thirty days. Suddenly, the remains were found on the shore, notifying the Chonghai Qiwu County Association and Shen's relatives. Shen's family members were filled with both sorrow and joy, and could not bear to have the remains exposed for any longer. Hastily, the coffin was entombed at the Five County Assembly Hall on Xietu Road yesterday morning, and there was no time to invite friends and relatives widely. Thus, close friends Zheng Hongnian, Zhang Zhenxi, Wang Hanliang, Sun Zhenwu, Cai Jianqing, etc., and fellow villagers in Shanghai, recognizing Shen's service to society for more than twenty years, leaving behind an elderly mother and young children in impoverished circumstances, the sound of weeping was deafening at the time of the entombment. The Shen Zhuowu Funeral Office has been set to hold a memorial service at the Jade Buddha Temple on the 30th. Shen's relatives and friends also plan to discuss all funeral arrangements and aftercare.

Kidnapping Case in Japanese-Occupied Area 113

Kidnappers and Japanese Soldiers Exchange Fire

The Continental Daily reported that yesterday (the 25th) morning, there was a sudden incident in Zhabei Qiujiang Road in which kidnappers and Japanese soldiers exchanged gunfire. It is heard that the victim, Chen Ruiwu (transliteration), is the owner of a restaurant on Suzhou Road and was shot and injured. As for the details, a reporter inquired with Japanese officers yesterday, and it was claimed that no detailed report has been received yet. However, according to the investigation by the Continental Daily, at around 9:00 AM yesterday morning, Chen was on his way to visit a friend on Qiujiang Road when suddenly seven bandits came forward, grabbed him into a car, and rushed to Zhabei via North Sichuan Road and Qiujiang Road. When passing Qiujiang Road, the Japanese soldiers ordered the car to stop for questioning. The driver answered in Japanese, claiming to be returning to his residence in Zhabei, and was released. Chen, seeing the situation, immediately cried for help. The Japanese soldiers shouted at the car to stop, but the driver accelerated and sped forward. At the same time, two bandits in the car opened fire on the Japanese soldiers, and the Japanese soldiers returned fire. It is believed that the driver was hit, as the car suddenly stopped. One bandit jumped from the rear to the front and pushed the driver away, taking over the wheel and driving away. Chen was seen attempting to escape, but was shot by a bandit and fell into the car. At this time, the Japanese soldiers continued to chase and fire, firing a total of more than forty bullets. However, due to the car's extreme speed, it eventually escaped. It is claimed that the car has a Zhabei business license plate number.

Anhui Natives in Shanghai Request Abolition of Harsh Taxes 114

The Shanghai Anhui Review Monthly Magazine, founded by Anhui natives in Shanghai, telegraphed Wu Zhongxin, etc., stating: "To Wu, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, Luo, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, He, Director of the Department of Finance, Cheng, Director of the Department of Construction, and all members including Zhang Wujiangguang: Our Anhui is suffering from harsh taxes. Placed in a state of misery, the people have been exhausted. Anhui people have been making rescue efforts in the province for years, exhausting their minds and efforts, hoping to relieve the distress. Last winter, the joint office of various Anhui associations abroad published a notice to the Anhui people, stating that all taxes and illegal levies created by Chen Diaoyuan should not be paid. The paper was full of agitation, hoping to solicit attention and correction. Now, fortunately, the central government cares about the people and has specially appointed you to return to Anhui to govern. At first, it was thought that you would surely reverse what Chen Diaoyuan had done and first abolish all illegal harsh taxes to alleviate the people's difficulties. Recently, on the 24th of this month, a Shanghai newspaper reported that Anhui Province's special business taxes on bamboo, wood, tea, hemp, silk, cocoons, food, oil, cotton, paper, and other categories will not be discontinued due to the reorganization of the provincial government, and will not be ceased despite merchants' opposition. Upon investigation, this kind of special tax is more harmful than Likin. As many as twenty-seven bureaus have been established. The extraction tax is layered, and the tax rate is as high as twenty to fifty per thousand, calculated on quantity and value. How can merchants bear this? At a time when bandits and communists are rampant and all industries are depressed, if we continue to collect taxes, then Chen Diaoyuan created it, and you will enjoy its success. It is foreseeable that production will be slow and sales will be difficult, and the people will be increasingly impoverished. The three thousand people of Anhui will not die under the military warlord's boots, but instead will die under the hands of Anhui people governing Anhui. You love your hometown, how can you bear to do this? We specially send this telegram and respectfully request that you resolutely abolish the taxes to console the people's expectations. We earnestly express our request, awaiting your order. Shanghai Anhui Review Monthly Magazine."

Taxi Stand Problem 115

The local taxi association had requested that the Public Works Department allow taxis to park near theaters, restaurants, and hotels, because public buses had already been granted the right to park near cinemas. Recently, the Deputy Secretary of the Public Works Department replied to the association, stating that public buses drive after the end of performances at the Picardie, New Light, and Guangling theaters, and park at designated locations, not at the entrance of the theaters. This is to provide cheap fares for the public, so it does not affect the business of taxis. In addition, there are taxi companies near each of these theaters. If other companies are allowed to park outside the theaters and solicit passengers, then these companies will definitely protest first. The space required for public buses to park three vehicles near the theaters is not much. Public buses must also operate in an orderly manner and not honk their horns to attract customers. If taxis are allowed to gather at entertainment venues, then the drivers and their assistants will inevitably honk their horns excessively, which will disturb the public, and it will be extremely difficult for the police to manage. Therefore, the Public Works Department does not want to approve the request.

The Tragic Situation is Unbearable to Read

The local Chinese Jisheng Society reports that, according to Zhai Fengxiang, director of the Anhui disaster relief office in southern Anhui, the disaster situation in Xuan Cheng, Fanchang, Nanling, and other counties is extremely severe. Although the disaster situation was relieved via our associations and the Emergency Water Disaster Association, since the beginning of spring, people have been starving to death. Root bark and tree bark have been eaten completely. There was a case where several dozen copper coins were given to a young child to buy food on the street, while the entire family committed suicide by poison. The situation of tragic deaths in various counties and villages is everywhere and endless. According to reports from Wuhu, the average disaster victim is unable to feed their fill or cover their body. They barely maintain their lives. They lack the oxen to plow and have no seeds to sow. In the past, they could sell their wives and children, but now, there is no one to ask about wives and children. They will either starve to death. There is no way to live and no solution to be found. According to reports, in Gaoxing village of the west ling section of Siyang County, Jiangsu, a family of thirteen committed suicide because they ran out of food and had no way to borrow. In addition, the director of the Henan relief office of the association, after returning to Shanghai from Henan, stated that the tragic disaster in southern Henan, etc., the villagers were starving and unable to bear it. The wheat has been exhausted, and the wheat harvest is hopeless. There is no place to die and those who are not going to risk it are few, and so on. Other demands for relief are coming in like snowflakes and cannot be met. The disaster situation is extremely severe after the local war. There are disaster victims everywhere in Taicang, Liuhe, Kunshan, Changshu, etc. Relief is not enough. The higher refugee, without food or clothing, is scattering. In addition to the shelters that have been temporarily allocated, there are countless awaiting rescue. The disaster in other provinces and counties is like this. The disaster near this port is like that. During this great calamity, deaths follow in quick succession. I hope people can make up their minds to save money and all kinds of expenses in order to save the disaster and clear up the hidden dangers.

Judgement in the 460,000 Yuan Embezzlement Case 121

Tang Shenyu Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment

In October of the 19th year of the Republic of China, Chen Zhusun, Tang Shenyu, Zhu Yougui, and four others raised 20,000 yuan to open the Zhenda Company at 392 Nanjing Road, specializing in stocks and government bonds. Tang and Zhu served as the general manager and deputy general manager, respectively. After starting operations, Tang and Zhu privately established four accounts under the names Yuji, Boji, Wenji, and Baoji, engaging in excessive trading, resulting in significant losses over the years. They secretly sold all the bonds deposited by customers with Zhenda Company to cover the losses. Recently, as the losses increased and could not be sustained, Zhu fled, and Zhenda Company went bankrupt. It is currently being liquidated. Tang Shenyu, upon the company's bankruptcy, reported to shareholder Chen Zhusun, who hired lawyer Wu Linkun to report to the Lao Zha Police Station. Western detective Hao'er and Chinese detective Lang Chengpei arrested Tang. Qing Qingren, the company's bookkeeper, Li Tairan, was also arrested as a suspect in the joint malfeasance. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division. Attorney Li Zhishan of the police station and attorney Wu Linkun, representing Chen Zhusun, successively stated that the defendants jointly concealed accounts and embezzled public funds amounting to 466,115.35 yuan. However, this was the amount admitted by the defendants and only a rough estimate. The actual amount may not be determined for some time. When questioned, the defendant Tang Shenyu confessed that Zhu Yougui, who is still at large, was the instigator of the matter. Li Tairan claimed to have no involvement. Judge Zhou Hanting reviewed the confessions and sentenced Tang to two years imprisonment. Li was found not guilty. Detention will continue during the appeal period. The ancillary civil lawsuit was transferred to the Civil Division for trial.

Drinking Bean Curd Jelly Causes a Death 122

Police Officer Luo Bin Remanded

The Case is Scheduled for Sentencing

Police officer Luo Bin of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, on the night of the 13th of this month, sought bean curd jelly to warm himself at the bean curd shop opened by Li Wenqing at 12 Kangjia Lane, Xiaodongmen. He had a quarrel with the shop assistant Liang Zaifu, who was from Chongming. In a fit of anger, Luo repeatedly struck Liang in the lower body with the barrel of his gun, injuring his kidney sinews. At that time, Luo was seized and escorted to the First District, Second Precinct and then to the District Court, where the injury was confirmed. Prosecution was initiated, but unexpectedly, Liang's injuries proved fatal. He died in hospital without responding to treatment. After further examination by the court, the nature of the charges were amended and yesterday morning, Judge Qian Chengjun held a court hearing. The defendant Luo Bin stated that he did not know Liang Zaifu. At three o'clock on the night of the 13th, while eating bean curd jelly, he struck Liang with the butt of his gun because the deceased had cursed him first. He did not expect the injury to be so severe, and it was too late for regrets. He had only been a policeman for two months, and he had no hatred for the deceased, and he did not act deliberately. Li Wenqing, the owner of the bean curd shop, stated that Luo Bin was a patron, and there was no hatred between him and the deceased. At three o'clock on the night of the 13th, the defendant came to eat bean curd jelly. When apprentice Shi Ruilang replied that it was not ready yet, the defendant hit the apprentice on the head. Liang Zaifu came to advise, saying that people should treat each other politely. He then struck Liang Yaofu with his gun. I was already asleep at the time, and Shi Ruilang and others told me about it afterwards. Liang died in Guangci Hospital at four o'clock in the afternoon of the 16th. Shi Ruilang stated that he was an apprentice. There were two shop assistants in the shop, one was Shi Ruiqing, and the other was Liang Zaifu. The police officer came to eat bean curd jelly and asked me for it. I said it wasn't ready and immediately slapped me. Liang Zaifu then said that other brothers were polite, why were you unreasonable? He then struck Liang Zaifu on the left side of his lower body with his gun. The second time Liang grabbed it, dragged him outside, and slapped him twice, etc. Shi Ruiqing stated that he was a bean curd shop assistant, and the rest was the same as what Shi Ruiqing said. The judge then asked if he was taken to the police station at that time, and answered that martial law was in effect at that time, and the police were not called until the next day. At this point, Prosecutor Yang was invited to the court to state his opinion. Appointed defense lawyer Hu Yuanjun defended according to precedent. The court then announced the conclusion of the debate, scheduled the sentencing for a later date, and remanded the defendant.

The City's Military Hospital Will Close 123

Plans to Create a Civilian Hospital

After the start of the Sino-Japanese War in Shanghai, the people in the rear engaged in relief and assistance, and many military hospitals were organized and established for medical treatment. In addition to the wounded soldiers who have fully recovered and been discharged, there are still many who have not recovered and remain in the hospital. It is learned that in order to unify the organization of military hospitals, the central government decided to establish three large-scale military hospitals in Bengbu, Wuxi, and Hangzhou, and to concentrate the soldiers wounded in the anti-Japanese war in these three hospitals for medical treatment. It is stipulated that the wounded soldiers in Shanghai and the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road area will be treated in the Hangzhou Military Hospital. The wounded soldiers along the Beijing-Shanghai Road will be treated in the Wuxi Military Hospital. The wounded soldiers along the Jinpu Road will be treated in the Bengbu Military Hospital. The relocation has now begun separately. The original military hospitals in Shanghai will be closed in sequence depending on the situation of each hospital. Some people believe that it is a pity to abandon the equipment and medicines prepared by the military hospitals. Shanghai also feels the lack of civilian hospitals. Therefore, it is planned to initiate the organization of a civilian hospital and transfer all the equipment of the military hospitals to the civilian hospital for application. It is truly a win-win situation and is currently being planned. (Far East News Agency)

The Popularity of Pinghu Baiguo Dumplings 124

Pinghu flour foods and candies have long been famous throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River. It is now heard that the owner of the S.K.S. Family Food Company, based on his usual experience, has hired technicians from the area to supervise the production of Pinghu Baiguo dumplings, which are of good quality and taste. They are not only nutritious but also easy to digest, can be stored, and are suitable for eating in both winter and summer. They are truly a treasure among desserts. They are currently sold through the Lili Local Products Company on Nanjing Road, Zhejiang Road, and sales are quite extensive. They are often unable to keep up with demand.

Argument Concluded in the Case of a Daughter-in-Law Biting Her Mother-in-Law 126

Sentencing Scheduled for May 3

Old woman, Huang, a local resident of a flat in Kangjili Lane, Kanti Road, French Concession, is sixty years old this year. Her daughter, Cui Bao, also known as A Liu, is twenty-seven years old and works in the Maya Silk Weaving Factory. She has been in love with the company's accountant, Chen Qiao, for more than two years. Recently, they asked a matchmaker to arrange a marriage, and it was agreed that they would be married on the 11th of this month. Huang prepared generous wedding clothes, dowry, and ornaments for her daughter, worth more than 800 gold. Huang's eldest daughter-in-law, Ye Zhang, nicknamed "The Tigress," was jealous that her mother-in-law was spending huge sums of money to marry off her daughter. On the 7th of this month, she extorted 3,000 yuan from her mother-in-law without success, and harbored resentment. At ten o'clock that night, she sneaked into the room while Huang was asleep and bit Huang's lower body six times, biting off two pieces of skin and flesh, one of which had been dragged away and eaten by rats. Not satisfied, she burned more than 50 pieces of her young daughter-in-law Cui Bao's wedding clothes the next morning. Cui Bao reported to the French police, who sent detectives to arrest Zhang and seize the ash of the clothes, and escorted her to the Second Special District Court. The police prosecuted her for the crimes of injuring a close relative and damaging property under Articles 293, 298, and 382 of the Criminal Law. The case was detained in the detention hall for investigation. Details have been recorded in previous reports. Neighbors Lu Wenbing, Zhu Wang, Sun Yongxing, and Song Guojun all testified in court in this case. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wang 　Xu and Prosecutor Wu Xiaoke visited the First Criminal Court for a continued hearing. They first interrogated both parties. According to Ye Cui Bao, her elder sister-in-law injured her mother and burned her wedding clothes. She requested an investigation and compensation for the clothes, etc. The defendant still denied it in every possible way. The court ordered the debate to begin. First, the police lawyer Gu Shouxi argued that the defendant's crime in this case can be divided into two points: first, injuring a close relative, biting her mother-in-law's lower body six times; second, damaging her young daughter-in-law's wedding clothes. All witnesses have testified in court, and she should be punished according to the law. The defendant's side initially hired lawyer Peng Qixiu to defend, but Peng appeared in court yesterday and announced the termination of the mandate. Dong Banggan was temporarily hired as a defense lawyer. Subsequently, the prosecutor made a statement, stating that the defendant's crime was in line with items 1-7 of Article 20 of the Criminal Law, and the judge should make a judgment in accordance with Article 294 of the Criminal Law.

Finally, the attorney Ye Fokan, representing the plaintiff, supplemented his reference to the Criminal Law. The court declared the debate concluded, scheduled sentencing for May 3, and remanded the defendant.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong coast is cloudy and unsettled, with a cyclone due to the eastward movement of a low-pressure system that has just passed Mongolia. The Yangtze River basin and the coastline here are cloudy and rainy, with possible thunderstorms and lightning, and the cyclone is intensifying due to the northeastward movement of the low-pressure system passing through Jiangxi. In the coastal area south of Ma'an Island, the wind is variable and there is fog. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 68.0 and the lowest was 51.8. On the same day last year, the highest was 82.6 and the lowest was 53.8.

Letter 132

Editor,

Regarding the report of the Shibo (申報) newspaper, we, the World and China Society (世界與中國社), would like to clarify that the Wuxi Correspondent (無錫通訊) article on April 20 stated that "Ms. Tao Fanggu (陶方榖女士) was arrested after the post office found a copy of the World and China (世界與中國) magazine" (世界與中國雜誌), which led to her arrest. However, according to the facts, and according to the Shibo (時報) newspaper on April 10 and the Great Evening News (大晚報) newspaper on April 23, it was "China and the World" (中國與世界) that was found, not "World and China" (世界與中國). We checked and found "China and the World" (中國與世界) in the market and it is a small weekly magazine, while our magazine is published monthly with 100,000 to 200,000 words in each issue. The content and format are completely different. Moreover, our magazine is registered with the Ministry of Interior of the National Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government, and has been reviewed and approved by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang. The arguments are accurate and have always been praised by all parties. There is no suspicion of being reactionary. We are only concerned about the reputation and business development, so we specially commissioned your lawyer to send a letter to you, asking you to correct it immediately, so as not to mix things up and harm the business. We hope you will consider it, and please check and correct it. Sincerely, Shanghai News Agency Editor, Lawyer Chen Zhigao, April 25.

Wild Plunge in Foreign Silver, Approaching the 7 Qian Mark 133

The Trend Remains Unstable

Creating an Unprecedented Record

Recently, the price of foreign silver has been plunging since mid-month when it once fell to a low of 7 qian and 2 li. The authorities tried to raise the price, and tea merchants made some purchases, so it stabilized for the past ten days or so. In the past few days, due to weak confidence and sluggish sales, prices have continued to fall, surpassing the previous low. Yesterday afternoon, it actually approached the 7 qian mark, showing the courage to break through this mark, which is an unusual change in the market. Even the most experienced people have never heard of this situation before. The early market price yesterday was 7 qian and 1 li 5 hao, which was 2 hao 5 li lower than the previous day, causing alarm in the outside world. In the afternoon market, it suddenly fell another 1 li 2 hao 5 li, reaching only 7 qian and 0 li 2 hao 5 li, setting a new record low, which is definitely not a good thing for business. The amount of remittance drafts made was 745,000 in the morning market and 365,000 in the afternoon market. Cotton Yarn Exchange Council 137

Proposed six conditions

The Brokers Guild is still discussing items 1, 2, 6, and 3. The Cotton Yarn Exchange Brokers Guild received the six proposals from the council and convened a meeting at 3 PM yesterday to discuss them. Regarding the first proposal to increase special certificates for cotton yarn, it is difficult to comply. However, subsequently, the guarantee deposit should be changed to half cash and half substitutes. Regarding the second item, increasing commissions, this should be postponed due to the difficult times of national crisis. Regarding the sixth item, the cotton yarn grading table,

The appraisal period was previously checked every six months, now changed to three months, and a majority decision has not been reached. The above three items are still under discussion. The six conditions are attached below: (1) The market will open on May 2nd. However, for the sake of business safety, both buyers and sellers of cotton yarn should uniformly pay a special certificate cash deposit of 6 taels, and cotton should uniformly pay a special certificate cash deposit of 2 taels.

(2) It is proposed to increase handling fees after the market opens.

(3) The method of collecting guarantee deposits according to grade, which was previously drafted, is now planned to be implemented when the market opens.

(4) Improve handling procedures: A. Standardize forms, B. Organize the market, C. Facilitate procedures, D. Please cooperate in handling matters.

(5) This time, the reopened market will feature futures contracts, with terms temporarily from July to October, totaling four months. Cotton will be traded for seven, eight, and thirteen months.

(6) In order to improve the cotton yarn grading table appraisal period, the subsequent futures contract grading table will only specify the most recent three months.

Yarn Sales Only 450 Bales 138

20-count "Ren Zhong" yarn has fallen 18.5 taels from its peak.

The cotton yarn market is increasingly sluggish, and the situation is very loose. Business is quiet everywhere because of the unstable situation, tight credit, and difficult commercial activity. The goods from inland yarn factories are being shipped to Shanghai one after another, indicating the coolness of trade. Foreign yarn has also seen a sharp drop. There is no vibrancy along the Yangtze River, and there are many stockpiles in Hankou. The North China region is occupied by Japanese yarn. According to Tianjin brokerage firms, Japanese goods flood the market there, and prices are extremely accommodating, leaving no room for Chinese yarn. Therefore, judging from the overall situation, the future is still difficult to be optimistic about. However, continuous declines have already caused a considerable drop. 20-count "Ren Zhong" yarn has fallen 18.5 taels from its peak. The downward trend may temporarily stop. According to some, the rainfall in the four rural areas of Geng is still relatively even this year, and sales may improve later. In short, the unstable situation and stagnant finance are major obstacles to the yarn market. It is found that all firms bought a total of 450 bales throughout the day. Among them, fellow merchants bought 15 bales. Prices fell again by 0.05 to 0.1 taels. Ningbo buyers bought 20 bales, Tianjin buyers bought 110 bales, Shantou buyers bought 50 bales, Changsha buyers bought 20 bales, North China buyers bought 60 bales, inland buyers bought 65 bales, Wuhu buyers bought 5 bales. Shenxin factories are still releasing small quantities.

Silk, Tea, Seawater Salt, and Spring Silkworm Rearing Significantly Reduced 141

Rural economy declines... Silkworm egg prices are surprisingly cheap

Haiyan, Zhejiang is also a silkworm rearing area. Farmers in the surrounding villages regard sericulture as an important sideline. This year, the rural economy has declined significantly. There is nowhere to borrow funds for silkworm rearing. Only families with mulberry trees have reduced their rearing. The rearing volume has decreased significantly. Currently, after the second molt, silkworm egg prices are surprisingly cheap. In previous years, each sheet of eggs would sell for more than one yuan and several jiao. This year, it only sells for three or four jiao, and it's all on credit. The cocoon market this year is bound to be unusually depressed.

Zhejiang and Jiangxi Tea News 142

Fuliang green tea picked early

The southeastern villages of Fuliang, such as Nan'an Tan, Zangjia Wan, and Shixiang, produce abundant tea. In addition to supplying foreign companies to produce black tea every year, the rest is picked green and sold to shops. This year, there are fewer tea shops in northern and western Fuliang than in the past. Farmers are deeply concerned about narrow sales channels and low prices. They plan to pick and sell to shops early because early-picked tea is tender and easily welcomed by buyers, and high prices can be obtained.

Suichun new tea will soon be available

Green tea in Sui'an and Chun'an, Zhejiang, sprouts earlier than in Anhui due to soil conditions in recent years. This year, tea shops in both places are extremely eager because the tea stocks in Shanghai have been sold out, and foreign companies have very high demand. Although the banks have tightened foreign exchange, most shops rely on money shops for loans. There is no concern that tea export companies will not be able to obtain funds. Tea shops in Gangkou, Weiping, and other places are very enthusiastic, raising and transporting cash to prepare for the market. If the weather warms up in the near future, new tea can be harvested. Tea merchants from Anhui and Jiangxi plan to relocate there to set up business because Sui'an has convenient transportation and abundant tea production.
